We’ve built technology that helps people find great therapists with the first software-enabled national network of providers accepting insurance.\u0026amp;nbsp;\u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;p\u0026gt;1 in 4 people in the US have a treatable mental health condition, but the majority of providers don’t accept insurance, making therapy too expensive for most people. Headway is building a new mental healthcare system that everyone can access by making it easy for therapists to accept insurance and scale their practice.\u0026amp;nbsp;\u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;p\u0026gt;Headway was founded in 2019. Since then, we’ve grown into a diverse, national network of over 34,000 mental healthcare providers across all 50 states who run their practice on our software. The engineering team at Headway is a small (~85) but mighty team using technology to build that future (and have a fun time while doing it!).\u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;h3\u0026gt;Principles that guide us:\u0026lt;/h3\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;ul\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;li\u0026gt;\u0026lt;strong\u0026gt;Focus on the mission\u0026lt;/strong\u0026gt;: We view software as a means of effecting change in the world, not as an end unto itself. These teams are highly cross-functional, often working with partners across EPD, CX, Growth, Clinical teams, and other functions to understand the needs of our therapist users - both individual providers and group practices.\u0026amp;nbsp;\u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;p\u0026gt;As an engineering leader at Headway, you will be responsible for establishing and growing these pods through hiring, people development, and strategic planning. We’re a Series D company with over $325m in funding from a16z (Andreessen Horowitz), Accel, GV (formerly Google Ventures), Spark Capital, Thrive Capital, Forerunner Ventures and Health Care Service Corporation.\u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;p\u0026gt;We want your time here to be the most meaningful experience of your career. \u0026lt;strong\u0026gt;Join us, and help change mental healthcare for the better.\u0026lt;/strong\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/div\u0026gt;\u0026lt;div class=\u0026quot;p-rich_text_section\u0026quot;\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;p\u0026gt;\u0026lt;strong\u0026gt;About The Role:\u0026lt;/strong\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;p\u0026gt;As a leader within Headway’s Revenue Operations org, reporting to the Senior Manager of Revenue Operations, you’ll have the unique opportunity to build, shape, and lead an operational function directly responsible for unlocking Headway’s growth to drive provider activation, retention, and share of wallet.\u0026amp;nbsp;\u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;p\u0026gt;As Headway scales to deliver high quality behavioral healthcare for millions of people across the country, the complexity of the operational landscape within which we operate has also increased exponentially. We’re a Series D company with over $325m in funding from a16z (Andreessen Horowitz), Accel, GV (formerly Google Ventures), Spark Capital, Thrive Capital, Forerunner Ventures and Health Care Service Corporation.\u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;p\u0026gt;We want your time here to be the most meaningful experience of your career. \u0026lt;strong\u0026gt;Join us, and help change mental healthcare for the better.\u0026lt;/strong\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/div\u0026gt;\u0026lt;p\u0026gt;\u0026lt;strong\u0026gt;About The Role\u0026lt;/strong\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/p\u0026gt;\n\u0026lt;p\u0026gt;\u0026lt;span style=\u0026quot;font-weight: 400;\u0026quot;\u0026gt;As Headway works to build a new mental healthcare system that everyone can access, we’re facing unique operational challenges and opportunities that come with growing and scaling at an unparalleled rate. We’re pushing the boundaries of the existing healthcare system so that we can fulfill our promise to providers, patients, and payers to create access to high quality providers across the nation.
